The layout of the room is the same as the pictures provided by the hotel. The sun is very sunny during the day, and the sunshine is very sufficient. The outdoor swimming pool is very large and clean, but the indoor swimming pool is temporarily closed. We saw weddings in the hotel for two days, both indoors and outdoors. If there are problems with the cleaning of the room, I will communicate with the room service staff and deal with it quickly. It is recommended to add foam splicing cushions to the bottom of the ocean pool in the children's playroom. There are also some self-funded projects, such as children's painting and fishing. I rented a 30-minute double bicycle to go around the hotel. I can also go out of the hotel and ride along the beach. When I stepped on the beach behind the Tianhou Temple, there was no road, so I stepped back. It was exactly 30 minutes.
In general, the experience is still good. During the National Day, you don't have to squeeze with others outside, nor do you have to get stuck in traffic on the road. The subway can go directly to the hotel entrance, and you can have fun. I will also recommend friends to bring their children here to play, and I will choose this hotel next time.
